local function updateCharacter()
    character = player.Character or player.CharacterAdded:Wait()
    humanoid = character:WaitForChild("Humanoid")
    hrp = character:WaitForChild("HumanoidRootPart")
end

local function parseMoneyPerSec(text)
    local number, suffix = text:match("%$(%d+%.?%d*)(%a*)/s")
    number = tonumber(number)
    if not number then return 0 end
    if suffix == "k" then number = number * 1000
    elseif suffix == "m" then number = number * 1000000
    elseif suffix == "b" then number = number * 1000000000 end
    return number
end

local function findBestAnimal()
    local bestMps = 0
    local bestPart = nil
    for _, plot in pairs(Workspace.Plots:GetChildren()) do
        if plot:FindFirstChild("AnimalPodiums") then
            for _, podium in pairs(plot.AnimalPodiums:GetChildren()) do
                local spawnPart = podium:FindFirstChild("Base") and podium.Base:FindFirstChild("Spawn")
                if spawnPart then
                    local attachment = spawnPart:FindFirstChild("Attachment")
                    if attachment then
                        local animalOverhead = attachment:FindFirstChild("AnimalOverhead")
                        if animalOverhead then
                            local genLabel = animalOverhead:FindFirstChild("Generation")
                            if genLabel and genLabel:IsA("TextLabel") then
                                local mps = parseMoneyPerSec(genLabel.Text)
                                if mps > bestMps then
                                    bestMps = mps
                                    bestPart = spawnPart
                                end
                            end
                        end
                    end
                end
            end
        end
    end
    return bestPart
end

local function createESP(part)
    if espParts[part] then return end
    
    local highlight = Instance.new("Highlight")
    highlight.Name = "ESP_Highlight"
    highlight.Adornee = part
    highlight.FillColor = Color3.fromRGB(255, 0, 0)
    highlight.OutlineColor = Color3.fromRGB(255, 255, 0)
    highlight.FillTransparency = 0.5
    highlight.OutlineTransparency = 0
    highlight.Parent = part
    
    espParts[part] = highlight
end

local function removeESP(part)
    if espParts[part] then
        espParts[part]:Destroy()
        espParts[part] = nil
    end
end

local function updateESP()
    if not espEnabled then return end
    
    for _, plot in pairs(Workspace.Plots:GetChildren()) do
        if plot:FindFirstChild("AnimalPodiums") then
            for _, podium in pairs(plot.AnimalPodiums:GetChildren()) do
                local spawnPart = podium:FindFirstChild("Base") and podium.Base:FindFirstChild("Spawn")
                if spawnPart then
                    createESP(spawnPart)
                end
            end
        end
    end
end

local function startESP()
    espEnabled = true
    RunService.Heartbeat:Connect(updateESP)
end

local function stopESP()
    espEnabled = false
    for part, highlight in pairs(espParts) do
        highlight:Destroy()
    end
    espParts = {}
end

local function buyGrapple()
    pcall(function()
        ReplicatedStorage:WaitForChild("Packages"):WaitForChild("Net"):WaitForChild("RF/CoinsShopService/RequestBuy"):InvokeServer(itemID)
    end)
end

local function autoEquip()
    pcall(function()
        local character = player.Character
        local humanoid = character:FindFirstChildOfClass("Humanoid")
        if not (character and humanoid and humanoid.Health>0) then return end
        local currentTool = character:FindFirstChildOfClass("Tool")
        if currentTool and currentTool.Name==itemID then return end
        local backpack = player:WaitForChild("Backpack")
        local grappleInBackpack = backpack:FindFirstChild(itemID)
        if grappleInBackpack then humanoid:EquipTool(grappleInBackpack) end
    end)
end

local function fakeFire()
    autoEquip()
    local args = {1.9832406361897787}
    pcall(function()
        useItemRE:FireServer(unpack(args))
    end)
end

local function startFakeFireLoop()
    if fakeFireLoop then fakeFireLoop:Disconnect() end
    fakeFireLoop = RunService.Heartbeat:Connect(function()
        fakeFire()
    end)
end

local function startAutoFly()
    if autoFlyConnection then autoFlyConnection:Disconnect() end
    autoFlyConnection = RunService.Heartbeat:Connect(function()
        if not autoFlyEnabled or not hrp then return end
        
        local bestPart = findBestAnimal()
        if not bestPart then return end
        
        local targetPos = bestPart.Position
        local currentPos = hrp.Position
        local distance = (targetPos - currentPos).Magnitude
        
        if distance > 10 then
            local direction = (targetPos - currentPos).Unit
            if distance < 20 then
                direction = direction + Vector3.new(0, 0.3, 0)
            end
            hrp.AssemblyLinearVelocity = direction * currentSpeed
        else
            hrp.AssemblyLinearVelocity = Vector3.new(0, 0, 0)
            fakeFire()
        end
    end)
end

local function stopAutoFly()
    if autoFlyConnection then 
        autoFlyConnection:Disconnect() 
        autoFlyConnection = nil 
    end
    if hrp then
        hrp.AssemblyLinearVelocity = Vector3.new(0, 0, 0)
    end
end

local function startControlFly()
    if controlFlyConnection then controlFlyConnection:Disconnect() end
    
    local flying = false
    local bodyGyro = nil
    local bodyVelocity = nil
    
    controlFlyConnection = RunService.Heartbeat:Connect(function()
        if not controlFlyEnabled or not hrp then return end
        
        if not flying then
            flying = true
            
            humanoid.PlatformStand = true
            
            bodyGyro = Instance.new("BodyGyro")
            bodyGyro.P = 9e4
            bodyGyro.maxTorque = Vector3.new(9e9, 9e9, 9e9)
            bodyGyro.cframe = hrp.CFrame
            bodyGyro.Parent = hrp
            
            bodyVelocity = Instance.new("BodyVelocity")
            bodyVelocity.velocity = Vector3.new(0, 0.1, 0)
            bodyVelocity.maxForce = Vector3.new(9e9, 9e9, 9e9)
            bodyVelocity.Parent = hrp
        end
        
        local camera = Workspace.CurrentCamera
        local moveDirection = Vector3.new(0, 0, 0)
        
        if humanoid then
            moveDirection = humanoid.MoveDirection
        end
        
        local lookVector = camera.CFrame.LookVector
        local rightVector = camera.CFrame.RightVector
        
        local velocity = (lookVector * moveDirection.Z + rightVector * moveDirection.X) * currentSpeed
        velocity = velocity + Vector3.new(0, moveDirection.Y * currentSpeed, 0)
        
        bodyVelocity.velocity = velocity
        bodyGyro.cframe = camera.CFrame
    end)
end

local function stopControlFly()
    if controlFlyConnection then 
        controlFlyConnection:Disconnect() 
        controlFlyConnection = nil 
    end
    
    if hrp then
        local bodyGyro = hrp:FindFirstChild("BodyGyro")
        local bodyVelocity = hrp:FindFirstChild("BodyVelocity")
        
        if bodyGyro then bodyGyro:Destroy() end
        if bodyVelocity then bodyVelocity:Destroy() end
        
        humanoid.PlatformStand = false
        hrp.AssemblyLinearVelocity = Vector3.new(0, 0, 0)
    end
end

local function toggleInvisible()
    invisibleEnabled = not invisibleEnabled
    if character then
        for _, part in pairs(character:GetDescendants()) do
            if part:IsA("BasePart") then
                part.Transparency = invisibleEnabled and 1 or 0
            end
        end
    end
end

onof.MouseButton1Click:Connect(function()
    controlFlyEnabled = not controlFlyEnabled
    updateCharacter()
    
    if controlFlyEnabled then
        autoFlyEnabled = false
        stopAutoFly()
        onof.BackgroundColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(0, 150, 255)
        startControlFly()
    else
        onof.BackgroundColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(0, 100, 255)
        stopControlFly()
    end
end)

    upPressed = true
    while upPressed do
        if hrp then
            hrp.CFrame = hrp.CFrame + Vector3.new(0, 2, 0)
        end
        wait()
    end
end)

    upPressed = false
end)

        end

    end
end)

-- === CONFIG ===
local FILE_NAME = "GlobalTop3ExecutionData.txt"
local MAX_TOP = 3
local MINIMIZED_SIZE = UDim2.new(0, 200, 0, 40)
local FULL_SIZE = UDim2.new(0, 320, 0, 220)

-- Load data
local function loadData()
    if isfile and isfile(FILE_NAME) then
        local success, data = pcall(readfile, FILE_NAME)
        if success and data then
            local decoded = HttpService:JSONDecode(data)
            if decoded then return decoded end
        end
    end
    return { global = 0, games = {} }
end

-- Save data
local function saveData(data)
    if writefile then
        pcall(function()
            writefile(FILE_NAME, HttpService:JSONEncode(data))
        end)
    end
end

-- Current game
local placeId = tostring(game.PlaceId)
local gameName = "Unknown Game"
pcall(function()
    local info = MarketplaceService:GetProductInfo(game.PlaceId)
    gameName = info.Name
end)

-- Update count
local data = loadData()
data.global = (data.global or 0) + 1
data.games[placeId] = (data.games[placeId] or 0) + 1
saveData(data)

-- Top 3
local function getTopGames()
    local list = {}
    for id, count in pairs(data.games) do
        local name = "Unknown"
        pcall(function()
            name = MarketplaceService:GetProductInfo(tonumber(id)).Name
        end)
        table.insert(list, {id = id, name = name, count = count})
    end
    table.sort(list, function(a, b) return a.count > b.count end)
    local top = {}
    for i = 1, math.min(MAX_TOP, #list) do
        table.insert(top, list[i])
    end
    return top
end

local topGames = getTopGames()

-- Top 3 List
for i = 1, MAX_TOP do
    local yPos = 0.37 + (i - 1) * 0.12
    local rankLabel = Instance.new("TextLabel")
    rankLabel.Size = UDim2.new(1, -20, 0.12, 0)
    rankLabel.Position = UDim2.new(0, 10, yPos, 0)
    rankLabel.BackgroundTransparency = 1
    rankLabel.TextColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(220, 220, 220)
    rankLabel.TextSize = 14
    rankLabel.Font = Enum.Font.Gotham
    rankLabel.TextXAlignment = Enum.TextXAlignment.Left
    rankLabel.Parent = content

    if topGames[i] then
        rankLabel.Text = i .. ". " .. topGames[i].name .. " → " .. topGames[i].count .. "x"
        if topGames[i].id == placeId then
            rankLabel.TextColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(100, 255, 100)
            rankLabel.Font = Enum.Font.GothamBold
        end
    else
        rankLabel.Text = i .. ". —"
        rankLabel.TextColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(100, 100, 100)
    end
end

    else
        frame.Size = FULL_SIZE
        content.Visible = true
        minimizeBtn.Text = "−"
        minimizeBtn.BackgroundColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(255, 100, 100)
    end
end)

end

-- === RESET (Hold R) ===
local canReset = true
Mouse.KeyDown:Connect(function(key)
    if key:lower() == "r" and canReset then
        canReset = false
        task.wait(3)
        if Mouse.KeyDown then
            if delfile and isfile(FILE_NAME) then
                delfile(FILE_NAME)
                print("ALL DATA RESET!")
            end
        end
        canReset = true
    end
end)

print("Hold 'R' for 3s to reset | Click '-' to minimize | Drag to move")

corner.CornerRadius = UDim.new(0, 8)
corner.Parent = frame

-- Glow (UIStroke) – will be recolored each update
local glow = Instance.new("UIStroke")
glow.Thickness = 2.5
glow.Transparency = 0.6
glow.Parent = frame

-- Text label
local textLabel = Instance.new("TextLabel")
textLabel.Size = UDim2.new(1, -12, 1, 0)   -- padding
textLabel.Position = UDim2.new(0, 6, 0, 0)
textLabel.BackgroundTransparency = 1
textLabel.TextColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(0, 255, 0)
textLabel.Font = Enum.Font.Code
textLabel.TextSize = 18
textLabel.TextXAlignment = Enum.TextXAlignment.Center
textLabel.Text = "FPS: --"
textLabel.Parent = frame

--------------------------------------------------------------------
-- DRAGGING
--------------------------------------------------------------------
local dragging = false
local dragStart, startPos

frame.InputBegan:Connect(function(input)
	if input.UserInputType == Enum.UserInputType.MouseButton1
		or input.UserInputType == Enum.UserInputType.Touch then
		dragging = true
		dragStart = input.Position
		startPos = frame.Position
	end
end)

frame.InputChanged:Connect(function(input)
	if dragging and (input.UserInputType == Enum.UserInputType.MouseMovement
		or input.UserInputType == Enum.UserInputType.Touch) then
		local delta = input.Position - dragStart
		frame.Position = UDim2.new(
			startPos.X.Scale, startPos.X.Offset + delta.X,
			startPos.Y.Scale, startPos.Y.Offset + delta.Y
		)
	end
end)

frame.InputEnded:Connect(function(input)
	if input.UserInputType == Enum.UserInputType.MouseButton1
		or input.UserInputType == Enum.UserInputType.Touch then
		dragging = false
	end
end)

--------------------------------------------------------------------
-- FPS CALCULATION & UI UPDATE
--------------------------------------------------------------------
local lastTime = tick()
local frameCount = 0

RunService.RenderStepped:Connect(function()
	frameCount += 1
	local now = tick()
	local delta = now - lastTime

	if delta >= 0.2 then
		-- Calculate FPS
		local fps = math.floor(frameCount / delta + 0.5)

		-- Update label
		textLabel.Text = ("FPS: %d"):format(fps)

		-- Choose color (text + glow)
		local txtCol, glowCol
		if fps >= 60 then
			txtCol  = Color3.fromRGB(0, 255, 0)      -- Green
			glowCol = Color3.fromRGB(100, 255, 100)
		elseif fps >= 30 then
			txtCol  = Color3.fromRGB(255, 200, 0)    -- Yellow
			glowCol = Color3.fromRGB(255, 220, 100)
		else
			txtCol  = Color3.fromRGB(255, 0, 0)      -- Red
			glowCol = Color3.fromRGB(255, 100, 100)
		end

		textLabel.TextColor3 = txtCol
		glow.Color = glowCol

		-- Reset counters
		frameCount = 0
		lastTime = now
	end
end)

    end
    return t_
end)()

local Rd=(function(ie,Oe)
    ie=te(ie)

    local function zd(G,Ac)
        local md=(function(...)
            return{...},pd('#',...)
        end)

        S=(function(E,Ad,Kd)
            if Ad>Kd then
                return
            end

        end)
        local function uc(db,fa_,ia,le)
            local id,Wc,Lb,Yd,ub,V,Ae,Ob,yd,vc,Pa,sa,i_,Re,Sc,sd,Wb,Cd,U,Sd,Od,pc,r_,td;
